DDR 鍥轰欢鐗堟湰锛歳k3588_ddr_lp4_2112MHz_lp5_2736MHz_v1.09

U-Boot SPL (idbloader) 鐗堟湰锛�2017.09-g5f53abfa1e-221223

U-Boot 鐗堟湰锛�2017.09

  

loader: 鐢眃drbin, usbplug, miniloader鍚堝苟鑰屾垚鍙敤浜嶹indows RK鍗囩骇宸ュ叿浣跨敤鐨刲oader

Rockchip 棰勫彂甯冪殑浜岃繘鍒舵枃浠�, 鍖呭惈 ddr銆乽sbplug銆乵iniloader銆乥l31/op-tee锛歨ttps://github.com/rockchip-linux/rkbin

  

## Boot 娴佺▼

Rockchip 搴旂敤澶勭悊鍣ㄧ殑涓€鑸� boot 娴佺▼:

|   |   |   |   |   |   |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|Bootstagenumber|Terminology #1|ActualProgramName|RockchipImageName|ImageLocation(sector)||
|1|PrimaryProgramLoader  <br>涓荤▼搴忓姞杞藉櫒|ROM code|BootRom|||
|2|SecondaryProgramLoader (SPL)  <br>娆＄▼搴忓姞杞藉櫒|U-BootTPL/SPL|idbloader.img|0x40|pre-loader|
|3|-|U-Boot  <br>  <br>  <br>ATF/TEE|u-boot.itb  <br>uboot.img  <br>trust.img|0x4000|U-Boot锛歶-boot-spl.bin, u-boot.bin (鎴� u-boot-nodtb.bin, u-boot.dtb )  <br>  <br>ATF锛歜l31.elf|
|4|-|kernel|boot.img|0x8000|kernel锛欼mage/zImage, dtb|
|5|-|rootfs|rootfs.img|0x40000||

- 闃舵1鎬绘槸鍦� boot rom 涓紝瀹冨姞杞介樁娈�2骞跺彲鑳藉姞杞介樁娈�3锛堝綋鍚敤 SPL_BACK_TO_BROM 閫夐」鏃讹級

娉ㄦ剰3锛氬浜� trust 鏄� trust.img 鎴栬€� u-boot.itb锛宎rmv 7鍙湁涓€涓� tee.bin 鏃犺鏈夋病鏈� ta锛岃€宎rmv8 鏈� bl31.elf 鍜� bl32 閫夐」銆�

### The Pre-bootloader(idbloader)

idbloader.img鏂囦欢鏄竴涓� Rockchip鏍煎紡鐨勯鍔犺浇绋嬪簭锛屽亣璁惧湪SoC鍚姩鏃跺伐浣滐紝瀹冨寘鍚細

- 鐢� Rockchip BootRom 鐭ラ亾鐨� IDBlock 澶达紱
    
- DRAM init 绋嬪簭锛岀敱 MaskRom 鍔犺浇锛岃繍琛屽湪 SRAM 鍐呴儴锛�
    
- 涓嬩竴绾у姞杞界▼搴忥紝鐢� MaskRom 鍔犺浇骞跺湪 DDR SDRAM 涓婅繍琛岋紱
    

  

#### 鎵撳寘 idbloader

瀵逛簬SD boot 鎴� eMMC boot锛岄渶瑕佷竴涓猧dbloader锛坉dr 鍜� miniloader 缁撳悎浣跨敤锛夈€�

```Bash
tools/mkimage -n rkxxxx -T rksd -d rkxx_ddr_vx.xx.bin idbloader.img
cat rkxx_miniloader_vx.xx.bin >> idbloader.img
```

浠� U-Boot TPL/SPL锛堝畬鍏ㄥ紑婧愶級鎵撳寘 idbloader.img锛�

```Bash
tools/mkimage -n rkxxxx -T rksd -d tpl/u-boot-tpl.bin idbloader.img
cat spl/u-boot-spl.bin >> idbloader.img
```

  

#### 鎻愬彇 idbloader

```Bash
rkdeveloptool db rkxx_loader_vx.xx.bin
rkdeveloptool ul rkxx_loader_vx.xx.bin
```

  

### U-Boot

#### **鎵撳寘 uboot.img**

浣跨敤 Rockchip miniloader 鐨� idbloader 鏃讹紝闇€瑕佽蒋浠跺寘 u-boot.bin 閫氳繃Rockchip tool loaderimage杞崲涓哄彲鍔犺浇鐨� miniloader 鏍煎紡

```Bash

```

鍏朵腑 SoCs 鍙兘鏈変笉鍚岀殑 $SYS_TEXT_BASE銆�

  

#### **鎵撳寘 u-boot.itb**

浣跨敤 SPL 鍔犺浇 ATF/OP-TEE 鏃讹紝鎵撳寘bl31.bin銆乽-boot-nodtb.bin 浠ュ強 uboot.dtb 涓轰竴涓� FIT image銆傛偍鍙互璺宠繃鎵撳寘 Trust image 鐨勬楠わ紝骞跺湪涓嬩竴鑺備腑涓嬭浇璇� image 銆�

```Bash
make u-boot.itb
```

娉ㄦ剰锛氳灏� trust binary 澶嶅埗鍒� u-boot 鏍圭洰褰曞苟灏嗗叾閲嶅懡鍚嶄负 tee.bin锛坅rmv7锛夋垨 bl31.elf锛坅rmv8锛夈€�

  

#### **鐑у啓 u-boot.img**

MASKROM妯″紡锛�

```Shell

$ sudo rkdeveloptool db ../../u-boot/rk3588_spl_loader_v1.13.112.bin
```

### Boot from eMMC

eMMC鍦ㄧ‖浠舵澘涓婏紝鍥犳鎴戜滑闇€瑕侊細

- 鎶婄‖浠舵澘鍒囨崲鍒� maskrom mode锛�
    
- 鐢� USB 绾垮皢鐩爣杩炴帴鍒� PC 鏈猴紱
    
- 浣跨敤 rkdeveloptool 灏� image 涓嬭浇鍒� eMMC
    

浠ヤ笅鏄笅杞� image 鍒扮洰鏍囩殑鍛戒护绀轰緥銆�

灏� GPT 鍒嗗尯琛ㄤ笅杞藉埌鐩爣锛�

```Bash

```

- SPL锛�
    

```Bash

```

- miniloader锛�
    


### Boot from SD/TF Card

We can write SD/TF card with Linux PC _dd_ command very easily.

Insert SD card to PC and we assume the /dev/sdb is the SD card device.

鎴戜滑鍙互寰堝鏄撳湴鐢� Linux-PC 鐨� _**dd**_ 鍛戒护鐑у啓 SD/TF card銆�

灏� SD card 鎻掑叆 PC锛屾垜浠亣璁� /dev/sdb 鏄� SD card 璁惧銆�

- SPL:
    

```Bash
dd if=idbloader.img of=sdb seek=64
dd if=u-boot.itb of=sdb seek=16384
dd if=boot.img of=sdb seek=32768
dd if=rootfs.img of=sdb seek=262144
```

- miniloader:
    

```Bash
dd if=idbloader.img of=sdb seek=64
dd if=uboot.img of=sdb seek=16384
dd if=trust.img of=sdb seek=24576
dd if=boot.img of=sdb seek=32768
dd if=rootfs.img of=sdb seek=262144
```

涓轰簡纭繚鎷斿嚭鍓嶆墍鏈変笢瑗块兘宸插啓鍏� SD card 锛屽缓璁繍琛屼互涓嬪懡浠わ細

```Bash
sync
```

娉ㄦ剰锛氫娇鐢ㄤ粠 SD card boot 鏃讹紝闇€瑕佹洿鏂� kernel 鍛戒护琛屽埌姝ｇ‘鐨� _**root**_ 鍊硷紙瀹冧綅浜� extlinux.conf)銆�

```Bash
append  earlyprintk console=ttyS2,115200n8 rw root=/dev/mmcblk1p7 rootwait rootfstype=ext4 init=/sbin/init
```

鍦� u-boot 涓皢 GPT 鍒嗗尯琛ㄥ啓鍏� SD card锛寀-boot 鍙互鎵惧埌 boot 鍒嗗尯骞惰繍琛屽埌 kernel 涓€�

```Bash
gpt write mmc 0 $partitions
```

  

### Boot from U-Disk

瀹冧笌 boot-from-sdcard 鐩稿悓锛屼絾璇锋敞鎰� U-Disk 鍙敮鎸佺4闃舵鍜岀5闃舵锛屾湁鍏宠缁嗕俊鎭紝璇峰弬闃� Boot Stage銆�

濡傛灉 U-Disk 鐢ㄤ簬绗�4闃舵鍜岀5闃舵锛岃灏� U-Disk 鏍煎紡鍖栦负 GPT 鏍煎紡锛屽苟涓旇嚦灏戞湁2涓垎鍖猴紝鍐欏叆 _boot.img_ 鍜� _rootfs.img_ 鍒板畠浠搴旂殑鍒嗗尯锛�

濡傛灉 U-Disk 鍙敤浜庣5闃舵锛屾垜浠彲浠ョ洿鎺� _**dd**_ _**rootfs.img**_ 鍒� U-Disk 璁惧銆�

娉ㄦ剰锛氶渶瑕佹洿鏂� kernel 鍛戒护琛屽埌姝ｇ‘鐨� _**root**_ 鍊硷紙瀹冧綅浜� extlinux.conf)銆�

```Bash
append  earlyprintk console=ttyS2,115200n8 rw root=/dev/sda1 rootwait rootfstype=ext4 init=/sbin/init
```

##### 璋冪敤鍏崇郴

```Bash
$ cd u-boot
$ sudo make rk3588_defconfig
    
$ sudo ./make.sh CROSS_COMPILE=$SDK_DIR/prebuilts/gcc/linux-x86/aarch64/gcc-arm-10.3-2021.07-x86_64-aarch64-none-linux-gnu/bin/aarch64-none-linux-gnu-
    process_args  CROSS_COMPILE=$SDK_DIR/prebuilts/gcc/linux-x86/aarch64/gcc-arm-10.3-2021.07-x86_64-aarch64-none-linux-gnu/bin/aarch64-none-linux-gnu-
    prepare
    select_toolchain
    select_chip_info
    fixup_platform_configure
    select_ini_file
    
        ## 閫夋嫨 boot1 閰嶇疆
        NAME=`filt_val "CONFIG_LOADER_INI" .config`
            CONFIG_LOADER_INI="RK3588MINIALL.ini"
            CONFIG_TRUST_INI="RK3588TRUST.ini"
            INI_LOADER=$SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini
                LOADER1=bin/rk35/rk3588_ddr_lp4_2112MHz_lp5_2736MHz_v1.09.bin
                LOADER2=bin/rk35/rk3588_spl_v1.11.bin
            INI_TRUST=$SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKTRUST/RK3588TRUST.ini
    handle_args_late
    sub_commands
    clean_files
    ## 缂栬瘧 u-boot锛岀敓鎴� uboot.img
    make PYTHON=python2 CROSS_COMPILE=$SDK_DIR/prebuilts/gcc/linux-x86/aarch64/gcc-arm-10.3-2021.07-x86_64-aarch64-none-linux-gnu/bin/aarch64-none-linux-gnu- all --jobs=${JOB} 
    pack_images
        pack_fit_image ${ARG_LIST_FIT}
            ./scripts/fit.sh --ini-trust $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKTRUST/RK3588TRUST.ini --ini-loader $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini --chip RK3588
                ./scripts/fit-core.sh
                    fit_process_args  --ini-trust $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKTRUST/RK3588TRUST.ini --ini-loader $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini --chip RK3588
                    fit_raw_compile 
                        null
                    fit_gen_uboot_itb
                        ## 鎵撳寘 ATF/OP-TEE/U-Boot/dtb/MCU 鑺傜偣閰嶇疆鏂囦欢
                        ./make.sh itb --ini-trust $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKTRUST/RK3588TRUST.ini --ini-loader $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini --chip RK3588
                            pack_uboot_itb_image
                                arch/arm/mach-rockchip/make_fit_atf.sh -t 0x08400000 > u-boot.its
                                    arch/arm/mach-rockchip/fit_args.sh
                                    arch/arm/mach-rockchip/fit_nodes.sh

                        check_its u-boot.its
                        ../tools/mkimage -f u-boot.its -E -p 0x1000 fit/uboot.itb -v 0
                        ./make.sh loader $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini
                            pack_loader_image
                                ## 鎵撳寘ddr鍚姩鍥轰欢鍒癰oot1
                                scripts/loader.sh --ini $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini
                                    cd ../rkbin
                                    ## boot_merger 鎵撳寘 idbloader.img鏂囦欢娴佺▼锛�
                                    ## u-boot/tools/rockchip/boot_merger.c
                                    ## u-boot/tools/rockchip/boot_merger.h
                                    $SDK_DIR/rkbin/tools/boot_merger $SDK_DIR/rkbin/RKBOOT/RK3588MINIALL.ini
                                        bin/rk35/rk3588_usbplug_v1.10.bin > rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin
                                        ## ../tools/mkimage -n rk3588 -T rksd -d rk3588_ddr_lp4_2112MHz_lp5_2736MHz_v1.09.bin rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin
                                        bin/rk35/rk3588_ddr_lp4_2112MHz_lp5_2736MHz_v1.09.bin >> rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin
                                        bin/rk35/rk3588_spl_v1.11.bin >> rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin  
                                        
                                        ## $ $SDK_DIR/rkbin/tools/boot_merger unpack -i $SDK_DIR/u-boot/rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin -o $SDK_DIR/rockdev/MiniLoaderAll
                                        ## ********boot_merger ver 1.2********
                                        ## input loader is /home/pang/work/sdk/rockchip/firefly_itx-3588j/sdk/itx_3588j_firefly/u-boot/rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin
                                        ## output directory is /home/pang/work/sdk/rockchip/firefly_itx-3588j/sdk/itx_3588j_firefly/rockdev/MiniLoaderAll
                                        ## extracting entry=471,file=UsbHead.bin
                                        ## extracting entry=471,file=rk3588_ddr_lp4_2112.bin
                                        ## extracting entry=472,file=rk3588_usbplug_v1.bin
                                        ## extracting entry=loader,file=FlashHead.bin
                                        ## extracting entry=loader,file=FlashData.bin
                                        ## extracting entry=loader,file=FlashBoot.bin
                                        ## Info:Unpack loader ok.
                                                                                             
                                cd ../u-boot
                                mv $SDK_DIR/rkbin/rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin ./  
                                mv $SDK_DIR/rkbin/rk3588_idblock_v1.09.111.img ./  (鏂囦欢涓嶅瓨鍦�)                                   
                    fit_gen_uboot_img
                        ## ATF/OP-TEE/U-Boot/dtb/MCU 鑺傜偣閰嶇疆鏂囦欢鎵撳寘鍒� uboot.img锛�4Mb锛夊ご閮ㄥ苟鍋氬浠�
                        cat fit/uboot.itb >> uboot.img
                        truncate -s %4096K uboot.img
                        cat fit/uboot.itb >> uboot.img
                        truncate -s %4096K uboot.img                        
                    fit_gen_loader
                        null
                    fit_msg_uboot
                    fit_msg_recovery
                    fit_msg_boot
                    fit_msg_loader
## boot1(spl)                    
$ sudo ln -s ../../u-boot/rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin ../rockdev/MiniLoaderAll.bin  
## boot2(uboot)
$ sudo ln -s ../../u-boot/uboot.img ../rockdev/uboot.img
```

###### uboot.its

```Bash

/*
 * Copyright (C) 2020 Rockchip Electronic Co.,Ltd
 *
 * Simple U-boot fit source file containing ATF/OP-TEE/U-Boot/dtb/MCU
 */

/dts-v1/;

/ {
        description = "FIT Image with ATF/OP-TEE/U-Boot/MCU";
        #address-cells = <1>;

        images {

                uboot {
                        description = "U-Boot";
                        data = /incbin/("u-boot-nodtb.bin");
                        type = "standalone";
                        arch = "arm64";
                        os = "U-Boot";
                        compression = "none";
                        load = <0x00200000>;
                        hash {
                                algo = "sha256";
                        };
                };
                atf-1 {
                        description = "ARM Trusted Firmware";
                        data = /incbin/("./bl31_0x00040000.bin");
                        type = "firmware";
                        arch = "arm64";
                        os = "arm-trusted-firmware";
                        compression = "none";
                        load = <0x00040000>;
                        hash {
                                algo = "sha256";
                        };
                };
                atf-2 {
                        description = "ARM Trusted Firmware";
                        data = /incbin/("./bl31_0x000f0000.bin");
                        type = "firmware";
                        arch = "arm64";
                        os = "arm-trusted-firmware";
                        compression = "none";
                        load = <0x000f0000>;
                        hash {
                                algo = "sha256";
                        };
                };
                atf-3 {
                        description = "ARM Trusted Firmware";
                        data = /incbin/("./bl31_0xff100000.bin");
                        type = "firmware";
                        arch = "arm64";
                        os = "arm-trusted-firmware";
                        compression = "none";
                        load = <0xff100000>;
                        hash {
                                algo = "sha256";
                        };
                };
                optee {
                        description = "OP-TEE";
                        data = /incbin/("tee.bin");
                        type = "firmware";
                        arch = "arm64";
                        os = "op-tee";
                        compression = "none";
                        
                        load = <0x8400000>;
                        hash {
                                algo = "sha256";
                        };
                };
                fdt {
                        description = "U-Boot dtb";
                        data = /incbin/("./u-boot.dtb");
                        type = "flat_dt";
                        arch = "arm64";
                        compression = "none";
                        hash {
                                algo = "sha256";
                        };
                };
        };

        configurations {
                default = "conf";
                conf {
                        description = "rk3588-evb";
                        rollback-index = <0x0>;
                        firmware = "atf-1";
                        loadables = "uboot", "atf-2", "atf-3", "optee";
                        
                        fdt = "fdt";
                        signature {
                                algo = "sha256,rsa2048";
                                
                                key-name-hint = "dev";
                                sign-images = "fdt", "firmware", "loadables";
                        };
                };
        };
};

```

```Bash
$ rm -r /mnt/sdupdate
```

```Bash
$ cd u-boot
$ sudo fdisk -l
$ mount | grep /dev/sdb
$ sudo umount /media/pang/E421-C20B
$ sudo mkfs.ext4 /dev/sdb
$ sudo sgdisk -z -og /dev/sdb
$ sudo sgdisk --resize-table=128 -a 1 -n 1:262144:62564351 -c 1:media -p /dev/sdb
$ sudo sgdisk --resize-table=128 -a 1 -n 1:64:16383 -c 1:bootloader -n 2:16384:49151 -c 2:uboot_a -n 3:49152:57343 -c 3:misc -n 4:57344:253951 -c 4:recovery -N 5 -c 5:userdata -p /dev/sdb
$ sudo dd if=gpt of=/dev/sdb2 bs=32768 seek=0
$ sudo dd if=bootloader of=/dev/sdb1 bs=32768 seek=1
$ sudo dd if=../kernel/boot.img of=/dev/sdb3
$ sudo dd if=../device/xgrids/images/rootfs.img of=/dev/sdb4
$ sync
```

```Bash
+Building
+========
+
+Configure Buildroot using the default board configuration:
+
+  $ make hifive_unleashed_defconfig
+
+Customise the build as necessary:
+
+  $ make menuconfig
+
+Start the build:
+
+  $ make
+
+Result of the build
+===================
+
+Once the build has finished you will have the following files:
+
+    output/images/
+    +-- fw_jump.bin
+    +-- fw_jump.elf
+    +-- fw_payload.bin
+    +-- fw_payload.elf
+    +-- Image
+    +-- rootfs.ext2
+    +-- rootfs.ext4
+    +-- rootfs.tar
+    +-- sdcard.img
+
+
+Creating a bootable SD card with genimage
+=========================================
+
+At the current time the genimage utility used by Buildroot produces
+corrupt GPT partition images. This is documented here for future use,
+but at the time of writing does not work.
+
+Buildroot builds a SD card image for you. All you need to do is dd the
+image to your SD card, which can be done with the following command:
+
+  $ sudo dd if=output/images/sdcard.img of=/dev/mmcblk0 bs=4096
+
+Creating a bootable SD card with sgdisk
+=======================================
+
+Below are manual instructions to setup the SD card. These should be
+removed when genimage can be used instead.
+
+Create the partitions on the SD card:
+
+  $ sudo sgdisk -g --clear \
+        --new=1:2048:67583  \
+        --change-name=1:bootloader \
+        --typecode=1:2E54B353-1271-4842-806F-E436D6AF6985 \
+        --new=2:264192: \
+        --change-name=2:root \
+        --typecode=2:0FC63DAF-8483-4772-8E79-3D69D8477DE4 \
+        /dev/mmcblk0
+
+The first partition will contain the bootloader and kernel
+(fw_payload.bin). The second partition contains the Linux
+filesystem.
+
+Copy the bootloader and kernel to the SD card:
+
+  $ sudo dd if=output/images/fw_payload.bin of=/dev/mmcblk0p1 bs=4096
+
+Copy the rootFS to the SD card:
+
+  $ sudo dd if=output/images/rootfs.ext4 of=/dev/mmcblk0p2 bs=4096
+
+Booting the SD card on the board
+================================
+
+Make sure that the all DIP switches are set to the off position for
+default boot mode (MSEL mode = 1111), insert the SD card and power
+up the board.
```

u-boot/arch/arm/mach-rockchip/param.c

```Bash
int param_parse_atags_bootdev(char **devtype, char **devnum)
{
#ifdef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP_PRELOADER_ATAGS
    struct tag *t;

    t = atags_get_tag(ATAG_BOOTDEV);
    if (t) {
        printf("Get bootdev type: 0x%x\n",
                t->u.bootdev.devtype);          
        switch (t->u.bootdev.devtype) {
#ifdef CONFIG_DM_MMC
        case BOOT_TYPE_EMMC:
            *devtype = "mmc";
            *devnum = "0";
            break;
        case BOOT_TYPE_SD0:
        case BOOT_TYPE_SD1:
            *devtype = "mmc";
            *devnum = "1";
            /*
             * If preloader does not pass sdupdate value, we treat it
             * as a unknown card and call the rkimgtest cmd to find
             * out what it is.
             *
             * If preloader pass sdupdate value as an update card,
             * we just set "sdfwupdate" to bootargs instead of
             * calling rkimgtest cmd which consumes time.
             */
            if (t->u.bootdev.sdupdate == SD_UNKNOWN_CARD) {
                run_command("mmc dev 1", 0);
                run_command("rkimgtest mmc 1", 0);
            } else if (t->u.bootdev.sdupdate == SD_UPDATE_CARD) {
                env_update("bootargs", "sdfwupdate");
            }
            break;
            ...
}
```

  

u-boot/arch/arm/mach-rockchip/board.c

```Bash
static void cmdline_handle(void)
{
    struct blk_desc *dev_desc;

    param_parse_pubkey_fuse_programmed();

    dev_desc = rockchip_get_bootdev();
    if (!dev_desc)
        return;

    /*
     * 1. From rk356x, the sd/udisk recovery update flag was moved from
     *    IDB to Android BCB.
     *
     * 2. Udisk is init at the late boot_from_udisk(), but
     *    rockchip_get_boot_mode() actually only read once,
     *    we need to update boot mode according to udisk BCB.
     */
    if ((dev_desc->if_type == IF_TYPE_MMC && dev_desc->devnum == 1) ||
        (dev_desc->if_type == IF_TYPE_USB && dev_desc->devnum == 0)) {
        if (get_bcb_recovery_msg() == BCB_MSG_RECOVERY_RK_FWUPDATE) {
            if (dev_desc->if_type == IF_TYPE_MMC && dev_desc->devnum == 1) {
                env_update("bootargs", "sdfwupdate");
            } else if (dev_desc->if_type == IF_TYPE_USB && dev_desc->devnum == 0) {
                env_update("bootargs", "usbfwupdate");
                env_set("reboot_mode", "recovery-usb");
            }
        } else {
            if (dev_desc->if_type == IF_TYPE_USB && dev_desc->devnum == 0)
                env_set("reboot_mode", "normal");
        }
    }
}
```

  

杩欐槸鍥轰欢 U-Boot 榛樿鍚姩椤哄簭閫昏緫锛�

|   |   |   |   |
|---|---|---|---|
|浼樺厛鍚姩绫诲瀷|bootdev.devtype|devtype|cmdline|
|- 2|EMMC锛�1 << 1锛墊0|bootargs=storagemedia=emmc|
|4|SD0锛�1 << 2锛墊1|bootargs=sdfwupdate|

鍥犱负BOOTROM鍚姩椤哄簭鍥哄畾涓嶅彉锛孲PI NOR(0)-eMMC(2)-SD CARD(4) 鏀逛负 SPI NOR(0)-SD CARD(4) -eMMC(2)

```Bash
/* tag_bootdev.devtype */
#define BOOT_TYPE_UNKNOWN   0
#define BOOT_TYPE_NAND      (1 << 0)
#define BOOT_TYPE_EMMC      (1 << 1)  鏀逛负 (1 << 2)
#define BOOT_TYPE_SD0       (1 << 2)  鏀逛负 (1 << 1)
```

### 澧炲姞 rkdeveloptool

```Bash
## 涓嬭浇缂栬瘧rkdeveloptool 
$ git clone https://github.com/rockchip-linux/rkdeveloptool.git
$ sudo apt install build-essential libudev-dev libusb-1.0-0-dev dh-autoreconf
$ sudo autoreconf -i
$ cd rkdeveloptool
$ sudo CPPFLAGS="-I/usr/include/c++/9 -I/usr/include/aarch64-linux-gnu/c++/9" ./configure
$ sudo make 
$ sudo make install 

## 鐑у綍闀滃儚鑷砮mmc
$ cd rockdev
## step1: db 鍛戒护浣跨洰鏍囧垵濮嬪寲DRAM骞惰繍琛寀sbplug
$ sudo rkdeveloptool db rkxx_loader_vx.xx.bin

## step2: wl 鍛戒护灏嗛暅鍍忓啓鍏ョ洰鏍囷紝姝ゆ楠ゅ彲浠ラ噸澶嶅娆�
$ sudo rkdeveloptool wl 0x40 idbLoader.img
$ sudo rkdeveloptool wl 0x4000 uboot.img
$ sudo rkdeveloptool wl 0x8000 boot.img
$ sudo rkdeveloptool wl 0x40000 rootfs.img

## step3: 浣跨敤 gpt 鍛戒护閫氳繃parameter_gpt.txt鍐欏叆gpt琛�
$ sudo rkdeveloptool gpt parameter_gpt.txt

## 闀滃儚鍐欏叆瀹屾垚鍚庝娇鐢� rd  comamnd 閲嶇疆鐩爣
$ sudo rkdeveloptool rd


澶囨敞锛�
## ul 鍛戒护灏� idbloader 浠� rockchip loader 鍐欏叆 idb
# 浣跨敤 Rockchip miniloader 鏃讹紝 ul 鍛戒护涓� "wl 0x40 idbLoader.img" 鍛戒护鎿嶄綔鐩稿悓锛屼絾浣跨敤涓嶅悓鐨勬簮銆�
$ sudo rkdeveloptool ul ../u-boot/rk3588_spl_loader_v1.09.111.bin

## rkdeveloptool 涓殑 ul 鍛戒护(ul= wl idbloader) 涓� upgrade_tool 涓殑鍛戒护 
## (ul = db + wl idbloader + rd) 涓嶅悓
```

```Bash

dd of=/dev/sdb if=./partitions/bootloader bs=32768 seek=1;  ###flash offset [    0x8000] 
dd of=/dev/sdb if=./partitions/gpt bs=10485760 seek=0;  ###flash offset [         0] 
dd of=/dev/sdb if=./partitions/recovery bs=7340032 seek=4;  ###flash offset [ 0x1c00000] 
dd of=/dev/sdb if=./partitions/uboot_a bs=8388608 seek=1;   ###flash offset [  0x800000] 
dd of=/dev/sdb if=./partitions/misc bs=8388608 seek=3;  ###flash offset [ 0x1800000]

sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/gpt-0s-33s bs=512 count=34;   ###dump offset [      0x0] size [        17KB] 
sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/gpt-1s-33s bs=512 skip=1 count=33;    ###dump offset [       0x200] size [        16.5KB] 
sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/gpt-0s bs=512 count=1;    ###dump offset [    0x200]  size [        512B] 
sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/misc bs=512 skip=49152 count=40;  ###dump offset [ 0x1800000]   size [        20KB] 
sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/bootloader bs=512 skip=64 count=8192; ###dump offset [   0x8000]   size [         4MB] 
sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/uboot_a bs=512 skip=16384 count=16384;    ###dump offset [  0x800000]   size [         8MB] 
sudo dd if=/dev/sdb of=./dump/recovery bs=512 skip=57344 count=131072;  ###dump offset [  0x800000]   size [        64MB] 
```

  

  

```Bash
#!/bin/bash
#
#  for Lixel  RK3588 platform sdcard FW burning
#
#  creat by garrett <gang.pan@xgrids.com>
#
# 

set -e

g_script_dir="$(dirname $(readlink -f "${0}"))"
g_work_dir=$(cd ${g_script_dir}/../ && pwd)
. ${g_script_dir}/envsetup.sh

g_sd_dev=
g_sd_img=
g_burn_img=
g_auto_find=
g_quiet_mode=
g_userid=$(id -u)

usage()
{
    echo " "
    echo "USAGE: [-s] [-b] [-q] [-h]"
    echo "No ARGS means auto find tar ball and install sdupdate card."
    echo "WHERE: -s = firmware to be make sdupdate "
    echo "       -b = firmware to be burned"
    echo "       -q = Cancel interactive inquiry when formatting sdcard"
    echo "       -h = make sdupdate help"
    echo "EXAMPLE: sudo ${0} -c ./update_sdcard.img -f ./update_ab.img "
    exit 1
}

get_removable_device()
{
    local device=$1
    local file=
    local flag=
    local removable=
    local read_key=""

    msg "nomal+" "Scanning  removable block device..."
    for blknm in `lsblk -nld | awk '{print $1}' | grep -v loop`; do  
        file="/sys/block/${blknm}/removable"
        if [ -f "${file}" ]; then
            flag=`cat ${file}`
            if [ "${flag}" == "1" ]; then
                removable="/dev/${blknm}"
                eval ${device}=${removable}
                msg "nomal+" "[*] ${removable}"
                msg "nomal+" "Fond removable device (${removable})."
               break
            fi        
        fi        
        msg "nomal+" "  [ ] /dev/${blknm}"
    done

    if [ -z "${removable}" ]; then
        msg "err+" "Please insert your sdcard! exit(3)"
        exit 3    
    fi  

    if [ "${g_quiet_mode}" == "true" ]; then
        return
    fi
 
    while [ "$read_key" != 'y' ] && [ "$read_key" != 'Y' ] && [ "$read_key" != 'n' ] && [ "$read_key" != 'N' ]
    do
        read -p "Are you sure to format device '${removable}'? (y/n): " read_key
    done
    if [ "$read_key" = 'n' ] || [ "$read_key" = 'N' ];then
        msg "nomal+" "User cancel format device '${removable}' , exit(2)"
        exit 2
    fi
}

get_image_path()
{
    local extract_path=
    local tarball_path=
    local tarball_name=
    local target_tarball=
    local sel_target_img=
    local sd_img_tarball=
    local burn_img_tarball=

    if [ "${g_auto_find}"  == "true" ]; then
        for target_tarball in `ls -t "${g_work_dir}/*.tar*"`; do  
            if [[ ${target_tarball} =~ sd ]] || [[ ${target_tarball} =~ SD ]]; then
                g_sd_img="${target_tarball}"
                sd_img_tarball="${target_tarball}"
                msg "nomal+" "Fond make sdupdate tarball (${g_sd_img})."
                break
            fi   
        done

        for target_tarball in `ls -t "${g_work_dir}/*.tar*"`; do  
            if [[ ${target_tarball} =~ sys ]] || [[ ${target_tarball} =~ SYS ]]; then
                g_burn_img="${target_tarball}"
                burn_img_tarball="${target_tarball}"
                msg "nomal+" "Fond burning tarball (${g_burn_img})."
                break
            fi   
        done
    fi

    if [[ ${g_sd_img} =~ .tar ]] || [[ ${g_sd_img} =~ .tar.gz ]]; then
    if [ -L ${g_sd_img} ] ||  [ -f ${g_sd_img} ]; then
            g_sd_img="$(readlink -f "${g_sd_img}")"
            tarball_path="$(dirname "${g_sd_img}")"
            tarball_name="$(basename "${g_sd_img}")"
            extract_path="${tarball_path}/unpack/${tarball_name}"
            msg "nomal+" "Extract '${g_sd_img}' to '${extract_path}'..."
            delete_dir ${extract_path}
            tar xf ${g_sd_img} -C ${extract_path}
            local sel_target_img=$(ls -t ${extract_path}/*.img | head -n 1)
            if [ -n "${sel_target_img}" ]; then
                g_sd_img="${sel_target_img}"
            fi
        fi
    elif [[ ${g_sd_img} =~ .img ]]; then
        g_sd_img="$(readlink -f "${g_sd_img}")"
    fi

    if [[ ${g_burn_img} =~ .tar ]] || [[ ${g_burn_img} =~ .tar.gz ]]; then
        if [ -L ${g_burn_img} ] ||  [ -f ${g_burn_img} ]; then
            g_burn_img="$(readlink -f "${g_burn_img}")"
            tarball_path="$(dirname "${g_burn_img}")"
            tarball_name="$(basename "${g_burn_img}")"
            extract_path="${tarball_path}/unpack/${tarball_name}"
            msg "nomal+" "Eextract '${g_burn_img}' to '${extract_path}'..."
            delete_dir ${extract_path}
            tar xf ${g_burn_img} -C ${extract_path}
            local sel_target_img=`ls -t ${extract_path}/*.img | head -n 1`
            if [ -n "${sel_target_img}" ]; then
                g_burn_img="${sel_target_img}"
            fi
        fi
    elif [[ ${g_burn_img} =~ .img ]]; then
        g_burn_img="$(readlink -f "${g_burn_img}")"
    fi

    if [ ! -f "${g_sd_img}" ]; then
        if [ "${g_auto_find}"  == "true" ]; then
            msg "err+" "Not found make sdupdate image in '${sd_img_tarball}'! exit(4)"
        else
            msg "err+" "Specified make sdupdate image does not exist!(${g_sd_img})'! exit(4)"
        fi
        exit 4
    fi
    if [ ! -f "${g_burn_img}" ]; then
        if [ "${g_auto_find}"  == "true" ]; then
            msg "warm+" "Not found burning image in '${burn_img_tarball}'"
        else
            msg "warm+" "Specified burning image does not exist!(${g_burn_img})"
        fi
    fi    
}

make_sdupdate()
{
    local dev_name="$(basename ${g_sd_dev})"
    local cmd_file="$(dirname ${g_sd_img})/partitions/cmd4recovery"
    local parti_mnt=
    
    msg "nomal+" "Umount all partitions of '${g_sd_dev}'..."
   for parti_dev in `lsblk ${g_sd_dev} -nl | awk '{print $1}' | grep -v "^${dev_name}$"`; do  
        parti_mnt=$(lsblk -no MOUNTPOINT /dev/${parti_dev})
        if [ -n "${parti_mnt}" ]; then
            umount ${parti_mnt}
            msg "nomal+" "Umount '/dev/${parti_dev}' done."
       fi
    done

    parti_mnt="/mnt/sdcard"
    mkdir -p ${parti_mnt}
    rm -rf ${parti_mnt}/*

   msg "nomal+" "Format '${g_sd_dev}' device..." 
   mkfs.ext4 -F  ${g_sd_dev}
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Format '${g_sd_dev}' deivice failed! exit(5)" 
        exit 5
    fi
    msg "nomal+" "Unpack make sdcard image '${g_sd_img}'..."
    delete_dir "$(dirname ${g_sd_img})/partitions"
    ${g_script_dir}/updateEngine \
            --image_url=${g_sd_img} \
            --update=sdboot \
            --extboot=${g_sd_dev}
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Unpack make sdcard image '${g_sd_img}' failed! exit(6)" 
        exit 6
    fi
    if [ -f "${cmd_file}" ]; then
        msg "nomal+" "Flash partition images to '${g_sd_dev}'..."
        msg "nomal+" ">>>>>>>>>>>> flash command >>>>>>>>>>>>"
        while read line; do 
            msg "nomal+" "${line}"; 
        
        done < ${cmd_file}
        msg "nomal+" "<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<"
        sh ${cmd_file}
        msg "nomal+" "Flash done."
    fi
exit 0
```

```Bash
#!/bin/bash
#
#  Used for SD card FW burning on the Linux RK3588 platform
#  in the Ubuntu environment
# 
#  creat by garrett <gang.pan@xgrids.com>
#

set -e

g_script_dir="$(dirname $(readlink -f "${0}"))"
g_work_dir=$(cd ${g_script_dir}/../ && pwd)
. ${g_script_dir}/envsetup.sh

g_sd_dev=
g_sd_img=
g_sd_img_def="${g_work_dir}/prebuilts/update_sdcard.img"
g_burn_img=
g_auto_find="true"
g_quiet_mode=
g_userid=$(id -u)

usage()
{
    echo " "
    echo "USAGE: <-b> [-s] [-q] [-h]"
    echo "No ARGS means auto find tar ball and install sdupdate card."
    echo "WHERE: -b = firmware to be burned"
    echo "       -s = firmware to be make-sdupdate"
    echo "       -q = Cancel interactive inquiry when formatting sdcard"
    echo "       -h = make-sdupdate help"
    echo "EXAMPLE: sudo ${0} -c ./update_sdcard.img -f ./update_ab.img "
    exit 1
}

get_removable_device()
{
    local device=$1
    local file=
    local flag=
    local removable=
    local read_key=""

    msg "nomal+" "Scanning  removable block device..."
    for blknm in `lsblk -nld | awk '{print $1}' | grep -v loop`; do  
        file="/sys/block/${blknm}/removable"
        if [ -f "${file}" ]; then
            flag=`cat ${file}`
            if [ "${flag}" == "1" ]; then
                removable="/dev/${blknm}"
                eval ${device}=${removable}
                msg "nomal+" "[*] ${removable}"
                msg "nomal+" "Fond removable device (${removable})."
               break
            fi        
        fi        
        msg "nomal+" "  [ ] /dev/${blknm}"
    done

    if [ -z "${removable}" ]; then
        msg "err+" "Please insert your sdcard!"
        exit 1    
    fi  

    if [ "${g_quiet_mode}" == "true" ]; then
        return
    fi
 
    while [ "$read_key" != 'y' ] && [ "$read_key" != 'Y' ] && [ "$read_key" != 'n' ] && [ "$read_key" != 'N' ]
    do
        read -p "Are you sure to format device '${removable}'? (y/n): " read_key
    done
    if [ "$read_key" = 'n' ] || [ "$read_key" = 'N' ];then
        msg "nomal+" "User cancel format device '${removable}'."
        exit 1
    fi
}

analysis_images_path()
{
    local sd_img_tarball=
    local burn_img_tarball=
    local tarball_path=
    local tarball_name=
    local sel_target_img=

    if [ "${g_auto_find}"  == "true" ]; then
        for tarball in `ls -t ${g_work_dir}/*.tar* 2>/dev/null`; do  
            sd_img_tarball="${tarball}"
            tarball="$(basename ${sd_img_tarball})"
            if [[ ${tarball} =~ sd ]] || [[ ${tarball} =~ SD ]]; then
                g_sd_img="${sd_img_tarball}"
                msg "nomal+" "Fond make-sdupdate tarball (${g_sd_img})."
                break
            fi   
        done
        if [ ! -n "${g_sd_img}" ]; then
            for tarball in `ls -t ${g_work_dir}/../*.tar* 2>/dev/null`; do  
                sd_img_tarball="${tarball}"
                tarball="$(basename ${sd_img_tarball})"
                if [[ ${tarball} =~ sd ]] || [[ ${tarball} =~ SD ]]; then
                    g_sd_img="${sd_img_tarball}"
                    msg "nomal+" "Fond make-sdupdate tarball (${g_sd_img})."
                    break
                fi   
            done
        fi
        
        for tarball in `ls -t ${g_work_dir}/*.tar* 2>/dev/null`; do  
            burn_img_tarball="${tarball}"
            tarball="$(basename ${burn_img_tarball})"
            if [[ ${tarball} =~ sys ]] || [[ ${tarball} =~ SYS ]]; then
                g_burn_img="${burn_img_tarball}"
                msg "nomal+" "Fond burning tarball (${g_burn_img})."
                break
            fi   
        done
        if [ ! -n "${g_burn_img}" ]; then
            for tarball in `ls -t ${g_work_dir}/../*.tar* 2>/dev/null`; do  
                burn_img_tarball="${tarball}"
                tarball="$(basename ${burn_img_tarball})"
                if [[ ${tarball} =~ sys ]] || [[ ${tarball} =~ SYS ]]; then
                    g_burn_img="${burn_img_tarball}"
                    msg "nomal+" "Fond burning tarball (${g_burn_img})."
                    break
                fi   
            done
        fi        
    fi

    if [[ ${g_sd_img} =~ .tar ]] || [[ ${g_sd_img} =~ .tar.gz ]]; then
        if [ -L ${g_sd_img} ] ||  [ -f ${g_sd_img} ]; then
            g_sd_img="$(readlink -f "${g_sd_img}")"
            tarball_path="$(dirname "${g_sd_img}")"
            tarball_name="$(basename "${g_sd_img}")"
            msg "nomal+" "Extract '${g_sd_img}' to '${tarball_path}'..."
            tar xf ${g_sd_img} -C ${tarball_path}
            sel_target_img=$(ls -t ${tarball_path}/*.img | head -n 1)
            if [ -n "${sel_target_img}" ]; then
                g_sd_img="${sel_target_img}"
            fi
        fi
    elif [[ ${g_sd_img} =~ .img ]]; then
      g_sd_img="$(readlink -f "${g_sd_img}")"
    elif [ -f "${g_sd_img_def}" ]; then
        g_sd_img=${g_sd_img_def}
        msg "warm+" "Not find make-sdupdate tarball or image, use defualt image('${g_sd_img}')."
    fi

    if [[ ${g_burn_img} =~ .tar ]] || [[ ${g_burn_img} =~ .tar.gz ]]; then
        if [ -L ${g_burn_img} ] ||  [ -f ${g_burn_img} ]; then
            g_burn_img="$(readlink -f "${g_burn_img}")"
            tarball_path="$(dirname "${g_burn_img}")"
            tarball_name="$(basename "${g_burn_img}")"
            msg "nomal+" "Eextract '${g_burn_img}' to '${tarball_path}'..."
            tar xf ${g_burn_img} -C ${tarball_path}
            sel_target_img=`ls -t ${tarball_path}/*.img | head -n 1`
            if [ -n "${sel_target_img}" ]; then
                g_burn_img="${sel_target_img}"
            fi
        fi
    elif [[ ${g_burn_img} =~ .img ]]; then
        g_burn_img="$(readlink -f "${g_burn_img}")"
    fi

    if [ ! -f "${g_sd_img}" ]; then
        if [ "${g_auto_find}"  == "true" ]; then
            msg "err+" "Not found make-sdupdate image in '${sd_img_tarball}'! exit(4)"
        else
            msg "err+" "Specified make-sdupdate image does not exist!(${g_sd_img})'! exit(4)"
        fi
        exit 2
    fi
    if [ ! -f "${g_burn_img}" ]; then
        if [ "${g_auto_find}"  == "true" ]; then
            msg "warm+" "Not found burning image."
        else
            msg "warm+" "Specified burning image does not exist.(${g_burn_img})"
        fi
    fi    
}

umount_mnt_partitions()
{
    local dev_name="$(basename ${g_sd_dev})"
    local parti_mnt=

   for parti_dev in `lsblk ${g_sd_dev} -nl | awk '{print $1}' | grep -v "^${dev_name}$"`; do  
        parti_mnt=$(lsblk -no MOUNTPOINT /dev/${parti_dev})
        if [ -n "${parti_mnt}" ]; then
            umount ${parti_mnt}
            msg "nomal+" "Umount '/dev/${parti_dev}' done."
       fi
    done
}

writing_sdboot_partitions()
{
    local misc_img="${g_work_dir}/prebuilts/create-sdupdate-misc.img"
    local output_dir="$(dirname ${g_sd_img})/partitions"

    ## Unpack partition images to 'partition' folder  from make-sdupdate image
    msg "nomal+" "Unpack make-sdupdate image '${g_sd_img}'..."
    delete_dir ${output_dir}
    ${g_script_dir}/updateEngine \
            --image_url=${g_sd_img} \
            --update=sdboot \
            --extboot=${g_sd_dev}  1>/dev/null
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Unpack make-sdupdate image '${g_sd_img}' failed!" 
        return 1
    fi
    if [ -d ${output_dir} ]; then
        ## Replace misc files to support sdupdate
        if [ -f ${misc_img} ]; then
            cp -f ${misc_img} ${output_dir}/misc
        else
            msg "err+" "Not found '${misc_img}'!" 
            return 1
        fi    
        sync
        cp -rf ${output_dir}/* ${g_work_dir}/partitions/
    else
        msg "err+" "Not found updateEngine unpack folder '${output_dir}'!" 
        return 1
    fi

    ## Writing gpt patition table, bootloader, uboot, misc and recovery images
    msg "nomal+" "Select patitiones:"
    while read line; do 
        parti_file=$(echo "${line}" | grep -oP 'if=\K[^ ]+')
        parti_name=$(basename ${parti_file})
        msg "nomal+" "[*] '${parti_name}'"
    done < ${g_work_dir}/partitions/cmd4recovery
    msg "nomal+" "Writing sdcard..."
    sh ${g_work_dir}/partitions/cmd4recovery
    msg "nomal+" "Write completed."
    sync
}

writing_user_partition()
{
    local parti_dev="${g_sd_dev}1"
    local parti_mnt="/mnt/sdcard"
    local tag_file="${g_work_dir}/prebuilts/rksdfw.tag"
    local cfg_file="${g_work_dir}/prebuilts/sd_boot_config.config"

    mkdir -p ${parti_mnt}
    rm -rf ${parti_mnt}/*

    ## Format user partition
    mkfs.exfat ${parti_dev}
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Format '${parti_dev}' failed!" 
        return 1
    fi
    sleep .1
    ## Copy config files to user partition
    mount ${parti_dev} ${parti_mnt}
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Mount '${parti_dev}' to '${parti_mnt}' failed!" 
        return 1
    fi
    if [ -f ${tag_file} ]; then
        cp -f ${tag_file} ${parti_mnt}/
        msg "nomal+" "Copy '$(basename ${tag_file})' done."
    else
        msg "err+" "Not found '$(basename ${tag_file})}'!" 
        return 1
    fi
    if [ -f ${cfg_file} ]; then
        cp -f ${cfg_file} ${parti_mnt}/
        msg "nomal+" "Copy '$(basename ${cfg_file})' done."
    else
        msg "err+" "Not found '$(basename ${cfg_file})'!" 
        return 1
    fi   

    ## Copy firmware to user partition
    if [ -f "${g_burn_img}" ]; then
        cp -f ${g_burn_img} ${parti_mnt}/sdupdate.img
        msg "nomal+" "Copy '$(basename ${g_burn_img})' done."
    fi
    sync
    umount ${parti_mnt}
}

make_sdupdate()
{
    delete_dir ${g_work_dir}/partitions
    mkdir -p  ${g_work_dir}/partitions
    ## Umount all partitiones before format sdcard
    umount_mnt_partitions

    ## Format sdcard disk
    msg "nomal+" "Format '${g_sd_dev}'..." 
    mkfs.ext4 -F ${g_sd_dev} 1>/dev/null
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Format '${g_sd_dev}' failed!" 
        exit 3
    fi

    ## Clear MBR and GPT patition table
    msg "nomal+" "Clear patition table..." 
    sgdisk -Z -o ${g_sd_dev} 1>/dev/null
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Clear '${g_sd_dev}' patition table failed!" 
        exit 3
    fi

    ## creare MBR patition table, assign 1 user partition(range:128MB~Maximum available storage capacity)
    parted -s ${g_sd_dev} mklabel msdos mkpart primary ntfs 262144s 100%

    ## backup MBR patition table
    dd if=${g_sd_dev} of=${g_work_dir}/partitions/mbr bs=512 count=1;   ###dump offset [      0x0]  size [        512B] 

    writing_sdboot_partitions
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Create sdboot partitones failed!" 
        exit 3
    fi

    ## restore MBR patition table
    dd of=${g_sd_dev} if=${g_work_dir}/partitions/mbr bs=512 count=1;   ###flash offset [         0] 
    sleep .5
    ## Umount user partition
    umount_mnt_partitions

    writing_user_partition
    if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
        msg "err+" "Create user partiton failed!" 
        exit 3
    fi
    
    msg "nomal+" "Make sdupdate success."
}

if [ "${g_userid}" -ne 0 ]; then
    msg "err+" "Please run this program as root!"
    usage    
fi

while getopts "s:b:qh" arg
do
case $arg in
    s)
    msg "nomal+" "Get make sdupdate card image '${OPTARG}'"
    g_sd_img=${OPTARG} 
    g_auto_find="false"
    ;;
    b)
    msg "nomal+" "Get sdupdate fw image '${OPTARG}'"
    g_burn_img=${OPTARG} 
    ;;
    q)
    g_quiet_mode="true" 
    ;;
    h)
    usage
    ;;
    ?)
    usage
    ;;
    esac
done

get_removable_device g_sd_dev
analysis_images_path
make_sdupdate
```
